  <script>
    var ytpreload = ytpreload || {};
    ytpreload.SnapClassList = ['content-snap-width-1', 'content-snap-width-2',
                               'content-snap-width-3'];
    ytpreload.getSnapClass = function(guidePinned) {
      var SCROLLBAR_WIDTH = 21;
      var CONTENT_PADDING = 50;
      var GUIDE_WIDTH = 230;
      var SNAP_WIDTH_2 = 1056;
      var SNAP_WIDTH_3 = 1262;
      var screenWidth = window.innerWidth ||
          document.documentElement.clientWidth;

      var spaceForContent = screenWidth - SCROLLBAR_WIDTH - CONTENT_PADDING;
      if (ytpreload.usePinnedGuideStyle() && guidePinned) {
        spaceForContent -= GUIDE_WIDTH;
      }

      if (spaceForContent >= SNAP_WIDTH_3) {
        return ytpreload.SnapClassList[2];
      } else if (spaceForContent >= SNAP_WIDTH_2){
        return ytpreload.SnapClassList[1];
      } else {
        return ytpreload.SnapClassList[0];
      }

    };
    ytpreload.GUIDE_PINNED_CLASS = 'guide-pinned';
    ytpreload.GUIDE_VISIBILITY_CLASS = 'show-guide';
    ytpreload.usePinnedGuideStyle = function() {
      var screenWidth = window.innerWidth ||
          document.documentElement.clientWidth;
      return screenWidth >= 1251;
    };
    (function() {
      var htmlEl = document.getElementsByTagName('html')[0];
      var classList = [htmlEl.className];
        if (ytpreload.usePinnedGuideStyle()) {
          classList.push(ytpreload.GUIDE_PINNED_CLASS);
            classList.push(ytpreload.GUIDE_VISIBILITY_CLASS);
        }
        classList.push(' ', ytpreload.getSnapClass(
            true));
      htmlEl.className = classList.join(' ');
    })();
  </script>

    <div class="list-land" id="content"> 
     <!-- Main hero unit for a primary marketing message or call to action --> 
     <div class="row"> 
      <div class="span12"> 
       <h1 class="page-header">Staff Assembly</h1> 
      </div> 
      <div class="span12"> 
       <ul class="nav nav-tabs sub-nav tab4"> 
        <li class="active"><a class="" href="index.html">Overview</a></li> 
        <li class=""><a class="" href="steering-committee/index.html">Steering Committee</a></li> 
        <li class=""><a class="" href="events/index.html">Events</a></li> 
        <li class=""><a class="" href="resources/index.html">Resources</a></li> 
       </ul> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <!-- Example row of columns --> 
     <div class="row-fluid"> 
      <div class="span4 hero-unit"> 
       <p>We promote the interest and welfare of all staff employees at UCOP.</p> 
      </div> 
      <div class="span4">
       <p>The OP Staff Assembly supports UC's mission by encouraging communication between staff and the administration and other members of the university community on matters of interest to staff employees, in accordance with California laws and regental policy. <span>Our activities provide forums where staff at all levels can discuss issues of mutual concern, and offer opinions and recommendations on polices, processes and programs.</span></p>
      </div> 
      <div class="span4">
       <p>Led by a <a href="steering-committee/index.html">steering committee</a> of five to eleven employees from across UCOP's units and departments, the assembly also fosters an understanding of the universitys mission and UCOP's connection to UC campuses, hospitals and laboratories by providing networking opportunities to increase exchange of knowledge in all aspects of the OP community. <a href="about-the-staff-assembly.html">Read more</a></p>
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <div class="row"> 
      <div class="span4 blustripe"> 
       <h2 class="allCaps"> About the Staff Assembly </h2> 
       <ul class="dotted-list"> 
        <li> <a href="about-the-staff-assembly.html">Mission and role</a> </li> 
        <li> <a href="_files/by-laws.pdf">By-laws (pdf)</a> </li> 
        <li> <a href="steering-committee/index.html">Steering committee membership</a> </li> 
       </ul> 
      </div> 
      <div class="span4 blustripe"> 
       <h2 class="allCaps"> Events </h2> 
       <ul class="dotted-list"> 
        <li> <a href="http://events.berkeley.edu/index.php/calendar/sn/ucop.html?view=calendar&amp;timeframe=month&amp;filter=Secondary%20Event%20Type&amp;filtersel=1459">UCOP calendar</a> </li> 
        <li> <a href="events/index.html">Upcoming events</a> </li> 
        <li> <a href="events/past-events/index.html">Past events</a> </li> 
       </ul> 
      </div> 
      <div class="span4 blustripe"> 
       <h2 class="allCaps"> <a href="resources/index.html">Resources</a> </h2> 
       <ul class="dotted-list"> 
        <li> <a href="/navigating-ucop/index.html">Navigating UCOP: Quick reference guide</a> </li> 
        <li> <a href="http://ucop.edu/local-human-resources/op-life/staff-affinity-groups/index.html">Interest groups</a> </li> 
        <li> <a href="http://www.ucop.edu/cucsa/welcome.php">Council of UC Staff Assemblies (CUCSA)</a> </li> 
       </ul> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <div class="row less3 novrflw"> 
      <div class="span6 grybx"> 
       <h4>Contact us</h4> 
       <p>For comments and general information, please <a href="mailto:OPStaffAssembly@ucop.edu">email the OP Staff Assembly</a>&nbsp;or <a href="contact-the-staff-assembly.html">submit feedback</a>.</p> 
       <p>You can also view a contact list for current <a href="steering-committee/index.html">Steering Committee</a> members.</p> 
      </div> 
      <div class="span6 grybx"> 
       <h4>Meet with us</h4> 
       <p><span>The Staff Assembly meets the 2nd Wednesday of each month from 12:00-1:00 p.m.&nbsp; </span>Please check the&nbsp;<a href="http://link.ucop.edu/calendar/">UCOP calendar</a>&nbsp;for the meeting room.</p> 
       <p><span>Meetings are open to all staff members, who are welcome to bring their ideas forward and volunteer.</span></p> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
    </div>

      var SNAP_WIDTH_2 = 1056;
      var SNAP_WIDTH_3 = 1262;
      var screenWidth = window.innerWidth ||
          document.documentElement.clientWidth;

      var spaceForContent = screenWidth - SCROLLBAR_WIDTH - CONTENT_PADDING;
      if (ytpreload.usePinnedGuideStyle() && guidePinned) {
        spaceForContent -= GUIDE_WIDTH;
      }

      if (spaceForContent >= SNAP_WIDTH_3) {
        return ytpreload.SnapClassList[2];
      } else if (spaceForContent >= SNAP_WIDTH_2){
        return ytpreload.SnapClassList[1];
      } else {
        return ytpreload.SnapClassList[0];
      }

    };
    ytpreload.GUIDE_PINNED_CLASS = 'guide-pinned';
    ytpreload.GUIDE_VISIBILITY_CLASS = 'show-guide';

      var screenWidth = window.innerWidth ||
          document.documentElement.clientWidth;
      return screenWidth >= 1251;
    };

            <p class="html5-popup-side-right"> <button type="button" class="captions-settings-font-inc yt-uix-button yt-uix-button-default yt-uix-button-size-default yt-uix-tooltip" onclick=";return false;" title="Increase font size" role="button" aria-label="Increase font size"><span class="yt-uix-button-content">+ </span></button> <button type="button" class="captions-settings-font-dec yt-uix-button yt-uix-button-default yt-uix-button-size-default yt-uix-tooltip" onclick=";return false;" title="Decrease font size" role="button" aria-label="Decrease font size"><span class="yt-uix-button-content">- </span></button> Shortcut: +/- </p>

     <div class="span-6" style="margin-left: 1em; display: normal;"> 
      <a href="https://ucribm.ucr.edu/Paws/PAWS.html" target="_blank"> <img id="growlBtn" src="/Images/home/growl_login_btn_default.png" title="" onmouseover="this.src='/Images/home/growl_login_btn_hover.png'" onmouseout="this.src='/Images/home/growl_login_btn_default.png'" alt="Log into GROWL" /> </a> 
      <a href="http://rweb.ucr.edu/" target="_blank"> <img id="Img1" src="/Images/home/RWeb_login_btn_default.png" title="" onmouseover="this.src='/Images/home/RWeb_login_btn_hover.png'" onmouseout="this.src='/Images/home/RWeb_login_btn_default.png'" alt="Log into RWEB" /> </a> 
     </div> 
    </div> 
    <div class="span-18 last" style="padding-bottom: 30px;"> 
     <table style="width: 700px" cellspacing="2" cellpadding="0" align="center"> 
      <tbody> 
       <tr> 
        <td valign="top" align="left"> 
         <ol> 
          <li>Click <strong>Search/Modify Course</strong> at the CRAMS main menu to search for the course you wish to delete (see <a href="search-for-a-course.aspx">&quot;Search for a Course Guide&quot;</a>).<br /> <br /> 
           <table border="0" cellspacing="2" cellpadding="0" align="center"> 
            <tbody> 
             <tr> 
              <td valign="bottom" align="left"> <img border="0" hspace="0" alt="" src="../../images/course-mgt/greenarrow.png" width="45" longdesc="#" height="24" /></td> 
              <td> <img border="0" alt="" src="../../images/course-mgt/chapter10one.jpg" /><br /> </td> 
             </tr> 
            </tbody> 
           </table> </li> 
          <li>Enter the Subject Area, Course Number, and Course Suffix (if any) of the course to be deleted. Set the remaining fields as needed. Click Search Courses.</li> 
          <li>Double-click the version (usually the most recent) of the course to be deleted, or single-click and then click Select.<br /> <strong>NOTE: </strong>To <u>preview the course in form format before you delete it</u>, go to the very top menubar and click File and the Preview.Close the form to return to the database.</li> 
          <li><u>From the very top menu bar, click <strong>Tools </strong>and then<strong> Delete Course</strong></u>. Note that after choosing Delete Course, the Last Effective Quarter is automatically filled in with the quarter just prior to the quarter in which the delete will be effective. <p> <img src="../../images/course-mgt/chapter10two.jpg" alt="" border="0" align="center" /></p> </li> 
          <li>Complete the Justification and Approvals fields and modify the First Effective Quarter and Year and the second and thirdfields on the Other Courses/Programs page if necessary. However, do not complete the Cross-listed field until step 6 below. To modify or complete a field, do the following: 
           <ol style="list-style:lower-alpha;"> 
            <li><u>Right-click</u> in the field and click Modify. <br /> <strong>NOTE: </strong>Clicking on History displays the history of a field (all previous versions). The Compare option is available only on longer fields and is designed for use only with courses that have been returned to you by the Reviewer or an approver (see <a href="returned-courses.aspx">&quot;Returned Courses Guide&quot;</a>). <br /> <p> <img border="0" alt="" src="../../images/course-mgt/chapter10three.jpg" /></p> </li> 
            <li>Revise the field.</li> 
            <li>Enter the Field Justification if one displays and check spelling, if necessary.</li> 
            <li>Click OK to exit the field.</li> 
           </ol> </li> 
          <li><strong>If the course is cross-listed</strong>, and its <u>partner is also being deleted</u>, enter the partner's subject area, course number, and course suffix (if any) in the Cross-listed field (see instructions in <a href="cross-listed-courses.aspx">&quot;Dealing with Cross-Listed Courses Guide&quot;</a>, Creating and Revising Cross-listed Courses).<br /> <br /> Or<br /> <br /> If the <u>partner is not being deleted</u>, do not enter the partner's subject area, course<br /> number, and course suffix (if any) in the Cross-listed field; however, do state in the justification for the Cross-listed field that the partner is not being deleted (e.g., XXX- 000 is not being deleted).Also, notify the partner's department by E-mail that you have deleted your course and that they need to initiate a course change to uncross-list their course from yours.</li> 
          <li><strong>Save</strong> the course<strong> </strong>by clicking Save Work (top left of the screen).</li> 
          <li>To <strong>exit the course without submitting</strong>, click Menu (top right of the screen). However, tosubmit the course, skip step 8 and go to step 9.<br /> <strong>NOTE:</strong> To subsequently retrieve the course, access it through the Work-in-Progress Queue WIPQ) at the CRAMS main menu.</li> 
          <li>To <strong>proofread the course</strong>, click Proofread (top middle of screen) and use the form format that appears to proofread your input. Close the form to return to the CRAMS database and update the course if necessary.</li> 
          <li>To <strong>submit the course </strong>to the Reviewer (Registrar's Office), click Submit Course (top middle of screen). If you find you have submitted in error, call the Reviewer to have the course returned to you.<br /> <strong>NOTE</strong>: The Change Summary page and Preview format will show the Reviewer the fields that have changed from the last approved version.</li> 
         </ol> </td> 
       </tr> 
      </tbody> 
     </table> 
    </div>

     <!-- com.omniupdate.editor csspath="/z-omniupdate/css/content.css" cssmenu="" width="790" --> 
     <div id="omnicontent"> 
      <p>For information on WASC and the accreditation process, including the detailed requirements for the Institutional Proposal for Accreditation, see <a href="http://www.wascsenior.org/wasc/">http://www.wascsenior.org/wasc/</a></p> 
      <p>For a summary of the accreditation status of UC campuses, see<span style="text-decoration: underline;"> </span><span style="text-decoration: underline;"><a href="http://www.ucop.edu/acadinit/wasc/welcome.html">http://www.ucop.edu/acadinit/wasc/welcome.html</a></span></p> 
      <p>For information on WASC reaccreditation at the UC Berkeley campus, see <a href="http://education.berkeley.edu/accreditation">http://education.berkeley.edu/accreditation</a></p> 
      <p>For information on WASC reaccreditation at UC Davis, see <a href="http://wasc.ucdavis.edu/">http://wasc.ucdavis.edu/</a></p> 
      <p>For information on WASC reaccreditation at UC Irvine, see <a href="http://www.accreditation.uci.edu/">http://www.accreditation.uci.edu/</a></p> 
      <p>For information on WASC reaccreditation at UC Los Angeles, see<span style="text-decoration: underline;"> </span><a href="http://www.wasc.ucla.edu/index.shtml"><span style="text-decoration: underline;">http://www.wasc.ucla.edu/index.shtml</span></a></p> 
      <p>For information on WASC reaccreditation at UC San Diego, see<span style="text-decoration: underline;"> </span><span style="text-decoration: underline;"><a href="http://accreditation.ucsd.edu/">http://accreditation.ucsd.edu/</a></span></p> 
      <p>For information on WASC reaccreditation at UC Santa Barbara, see&nbsp;<a href="http://evc.ucsb.edu/wasc/">http://evc.ucsb.edu/wasc/</a></p> 
      <p>For information on WASC reaccreditation at UC Santa Cruz, see <a href="http://planning.ucsc.edu/wasc/">http://planning.ucsc.edu/wasc/</a></p> 
      <p align="right"><a onclick="window.scrollTo(0,0); return false" href="#">Back to Top</a></p>
